<!----> <!----></tbody></table></div></div> <article class=\"file-holder limited-width-container readme-holder\"><div class=\"js-file-title file-title-flex-parent gl-px-4 gl-py-3\"><div class=\"file-header-content\"><svg data-testid=\"doc-text-icon\" role=\"img\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"gl-icon s16 gl-fill-current\"><use href=\"/assets/icons-744c96d42bcc6345fdb1c870432a980c5f983ed177df344a4a5f94b625ac4ce8.svg#doc-text\"></use></svg> <a href=\"/sheeeng/magnolia1234-bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean/-/blob/master/README.md?ref_type=heads\" class=\"gl-link\"><strong>README.md</strong></a></div></div> <div data-testid=\"blob-viewer-content\" itemprop=\"about\" class=\"blob-viewer\"><div><div class=\"blob-viewer\" data-path=\"README.md\" data-rich-type=\"markup\">\n<div class=\"file-content js-markup-content md\">\n<h1 id=\"user-content-bypass-paywalls-clean-for-chrome\" data-sourcepos=\"1:1-1:34\" dir=\"auto\">Bypass Paywalls Clean for Chrome<a href=\"#bypass-paywalls-clean-for-chrome\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Bypass Paywalls Clean for Chrome“\" data-heading-content=\"Bypass Paywalls Clean for Chrome\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h1>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"3:1-5:52\" dir=\"auto\">Extension allows you to read articles from (supported) sites that implement a paywall.<br data-sourcepos=\"3:87-3:89\">\nYou can also add a domain as custom site and try to bypass the paywall.<br data-sourcepos=\"4:72-4:74\">\nWeekly updates are released for fixes and new sites.</p>\n<ul data-sourcepos=\"7:1-17:27\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"7:1-7:31\"><a data-sourcepos=\"7:3-7:31\" href=\"#installation\">Installation</a></li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"8:1-8:19\"><a data-sourcepos=\"8:3-8:19\" href=\"#update\">Update</a></li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"9:1-9:37\"><a data-sourcepos=\"9:3-9:37\" href=\"#troubleshooting\">Troubleshooting</a></li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"10:1-10:59\"><a data-sourcepos=\"10:3-10:59\" href=\"#list-of-supported-websites\">List of supported websites</a></li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"11:1-11:91\"><a data-sourcepos=\"11:3-11:91\" href=\"#sites-with-limited-number-of-free-articles\">Sites with limited number of free articles</a></li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"12:1-12:41\"><a data-sourcepos=\"12:3-12:41\" href=\"#new-site-requests\">New site requests</a></li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"13:1-13:37\"><a data-sourcepos=\"13:3-13:37\" href=\"#add-custom-site\">Add custom site</a></li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"14:1-14:41\"><a data-sourcepos=\"14:3-14:41\" href=\"#add-excluded-site\">Add excluded site</a></li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"15:1-15:43\"><a data-sourcepos=\"15:3-15:43\" href=\"#changelog-releases\">Changelog-releases</a></li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"16:1-16:21\"><a data-sourcepos=\"16:3-16:21\" href=\"#license\">License</a></li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"17:1-18:0\"><a data-sourcepos=\"17:3-17:27\" href=\"#disclaimer\">Disclaimer</a></li>\n</ul>\n<h3 id=\"user-content-installation\" data-sourcepos=\"19:1-19:16\" dir=\"auto\">Installation<a href=\"#installation\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Installation“\" data-heading-content=\"Installation\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h3>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"20:1-23:111\" dir=\"auto\">This extension is not available on the Google Chrome Web Store.<br data-sourcepos=\"20:64-20:66\">\nThe following instructions are needed to install third-party extensions in <a data-sourcepos=\"21:76-21:139\" href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chromium_(web_browser)\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Chromium</a>-based desktop browsers.<br data-sourcepos=\"21:164-21:166\">\nIn extension developer mode you can always install BPC by <code data-sourcepos=\"22:59-22:73\">Load unpacked</code> (latest master, but no automatic updates) or by crx-file (latest release &amp; automatic updates, but possibly you have to add the extension to the allowlist).<br data-sourcepos=\"22:230-22:232\">\nYou can add/pin the extension icon to the toolbar with the toolbar extensions menu (jigsaw puzzle shaped icon).</p>\n<h4 id=\"user-content-load-unpacked-chrome-ms-edge-or-brave-all-desktop\" data-sourcepos=\"25:1-25:58\" dir=\"auto\">Load unpacked: Chrome, MS Edge or Brave (all desktop)<a href=\"#load-unpacked-chrome-ms-edge-or-brave-all-desktop\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Load unpacked: Chrome, MS Edge or Brave (all desktop)“\" data-heading-content=\"Load unpacked: Chrome, MS Edge or Brave (all desktop)\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h4>\n<ul data-sourcepos=\"26:1-26:94\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"26:1-27:0\">or add extension to allowlist and install automatically updating crx-file (see next section)</li>\n</ul>\n<ol data-sourcepos=\"28:1-33:92\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"28:1-28:175\">Download this repository as a <a data-sourcepos=\"28:34-28:174\" href=\"https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean/-/archive/master/bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean-master.zip\">ZIP-file from GitLab</a>.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"29:1-29:91\">Unzip the file and you should have a folder named <code data-sourcepos=\"29:54-29:90\">bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean-master</code>.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"30:1-30:106\">Move the folder to a permanent location on your computer (do not delete the folder after installation).</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"31:1-31:53\">Go to the extensions page (<code data-sourcepos=\"31:31-31:51\">chrome://extensions</code>).</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"32:1-32:25\">Enable Developer Mode.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"33:1-34:0\">Click <code data-sourcepos=\"33:10-33:24\">Load unpacked</code> and select/open the extension folder (contains file manifest.json).</li>\n</ol>\n<ul data-sourcepos=\"35:1-35:309\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"35:1-35:309\">By default BPC has limited permissions, but you can opt-in to enable custom sites (and also clear cookies/block general paywall-scripts for unlisted sites). You can also just request permissions for the custom sites you added yourself (or <code data-sourcepos=\"35:243-35:257\">clear cookies</code> (BPC-icon) to ask for permission for current site).</li>\n</ul>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"37:1-37:151\" dir=\"auto\">If you're familiar with Git(Hub)-clients you can also clone this repo and update the extension that way (load unpacked folder used by Git(Hub)-client).</p>\n<h4 id=\"user-content-crx-file-other-chromium-browsers-operavivaldiyandex\" data-sourcepos=\"39:1-39:61\" dir=\"auto\">CRX-file: other Chromium browsers (Opera/Vivaldi/Yandex)<a href=\"#crx-file-other-chromium-browsers-operavivaldiyandex\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „CRX-file: other Chromium browsers (Opera/Vivaldi/Yandex)“\" data-heading-content=\"CRX-file: other Chromium browsers (Opera/Vivaldi/Yandex)\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h4>\n<ul data-sourcepos=\"40:1-40:177\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"40:1-41:0\">or add extension to allowlist for Chrome, MS Edge or Brave (see <a data-sourcepos=\"40:67-40:176\" href=\"https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean/-/tree/master/allowlist/README.md\">instructions</a>)</li>\n</ul>\n<ol data-sourcepos=\"42:1-45:182\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"42:1-42:167\">Download the extension as a crx-file (right-click &gt; save link as) from the <a data-sourcepos=\"42:79-42:166\" href=\"https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean/-/releases\">releases page</a>.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"43:1-43:69\">In your browser go to the extensions page (<code data-sourcepos=\"43:47-43:67\">chrome://extensions</code>).</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"44:1-44:25\">Enable Developer Mode.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"45:1-46:0\">Drag your crx-file anywhere on the page to import it (when you have an active 'load unpacked' installation, first remove it (and backup your custom sites); for automatic updates).</li>\n</ol>\n<ul data-sourcepos=\"47:1-47:308\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"47:1-48:0\">By default BPC has limited permissions, but you can opt-in to enable custom sites (and also clear cookies/block general paywall-scripts for unlisted sites). You can also just request permissions for the custom sites you added yourself (or <code data-sourcepos=\"47:242-47:256\">clear cookies</code> (BPC-icon) to ask for permission for current site).</li>\n</ul>\n<h4 id=\"user-content-android\" data-sourcepos=\"49:1-49:12\" dir=\"auto\">Android<a href=\"#android\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Android“\" data-heading-content=\"Android\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h4>\n<ol data-sourcepos=\"50:1-51:4\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"50:1-50:129\">Install <a data-sourcepos=\"50:12-50:102\" href=\"https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.kiwibrowser.browser&amp;hl=nl\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Kiwi Browser</a> from the Google PlayStore.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"51:1-51:24\">You have two options:</li>\n</ol>\n<ul data-sourcepos=\"52:1-53:166\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"52:1-52:161\">load the CRX-file in releases (auto-updating, no allowlist needed, opt-in for custom sites not working (use kiwi-custom crx; updates to latest regular version)</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"53:1-54:0\">install latest master zip-file (no automatic updates, for custom sites use manifest.json from custom folder, clearing Kiwi-cache will also remove extension though).</li>\n</ul>\n<h4 id=\"user-content-firefox\" data-sourcepos=\"55:1-55:12\" dir=\"auto\">Firefox<a href=\"#firefox\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Firefox“\" data-heading-content=\"Firefox\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h4>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"56:1-56:118\" dir=\"auto\">Visit the <a data-sourcepos=\"56:11-56:93\" href=\"https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-firefox-clean\">Firefox repository</a> of Bypass Paywall Clean.</p>\n<h4 id=\"user-content-iosipados\" data-sourcepos=\"58:1-58:15\" dir=\"auto\">iOS/iPadOS<a href=\"#iosipados\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „iOS/iPadOS“\" data-heading-content=\"iOS/iPadOS\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h4>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"59:1-59:104\" dir=\"auto\">Use adblocker with custom (content)filter: <a data-sourcepos=\"59:44-59:104\" href=\"https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-clean-filters\">https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-clean-filters</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"user-content-update\" data-sourcepos=\"61:1-61:10\" dir=\"auto\">Update<a href=\"#update\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Update“\" data-heading-content=\"Update\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h3>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"62:1-65:116\" dir=\"auto\">For crx-installation: check for updates (in <a data-sourcepos=\"62:45-62:66\" href=\"chrome://extensions).%5C\">chrome://extensions).\\</a>\nFor zip-installation (load unpacked/developer mode): unzip files to installation folder or use a Git(Hub)-client to clone the extension (locally).<br data-sourcepos=\"63:147-63:148\">\nYou can also check for update of site rules at startup (opt-in); only available until about 10 days after fix-release.<br data-sourcepos=\"64:119-64:120\">\nFor new sites you also have to opt-in to custom sites/request permissions for new domains (or wait for new release).</p>\n<h3 id=\"user-content-troubleshooting\" data-sourcepos=\"67:1-67:19\" dir=\"auto\">Troubleshooting<a href=\"#troubleshooting\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Troubleshooting“\" data-heading-content=\"Troubleshooting\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h3>\n<ul data-sourcepos=\"68:1-76:340\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"68:1-68:101\">If a site doesn't work, first try to turn off your adblocker (or other extension) and refresh page.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"69:1-69:52\">Make sure the (new) site is checked under Options.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"70:1-70:101\">Clear cookies by extension's icon (popup) and grant permission for site (or opt-in to custom sites)</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"71:1-71:64\">You will be logged out for most of the sites you have enabled.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"72:1-72:71\">Make sure you're running the latest version of Bypass Paywalls Clean.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"73:1-73:193\">Some sites need to redirect to an amp-page (add an exception in your <code data-sourcepos=\"73:72-73:93\">Redirect AMP to HTML</code> or <code data-sourcepos=\"73:98-73:128\">DuckDuckGo Privacy Essentials</code> extension or disable Brave &gt; Shields &gt; Auto-redirect AMP pages).</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"74:1-74:122\">If none of these work, you can <a data-sourcepos=\"74:34-74:121\" href=\"https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean/-/issues\">submit an issue</a>.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"75:1-75:158\">This extension works best alongside the adblocker <a data-sourcepos=\"75:53-75:157\" href=\"https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/ublock-origin/cjpalhdlnbpafiamejdnhcphjbkeiagm\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">uBlock Origin</a>.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"76:1-77:0\">If you live in the EU, also consider adding these filters to your adblocker (in order to remove cookie warnings): <a data-sourcepos=\"76:117-76:188\" href=\"https://secure.fanboy.co.nz/fanboy-cookiemonster.txt\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Easylist Cookies</a> | <a data-sourcepos=\"76:192-76:279\" href=\"https://www.i-dont-care-about-cookies.eu/abp\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">I don't care about cookies custom filter</a>. Some sites need to set a consent-cookie for (social) media.</li>\n</ul>\n<h3 id=\"user-content-list-of-supported-websites\" data-sourcepos=\"78:1-78:30\" dir=\"auto\">List of supported websites<a noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Diario Correo</a> -\n<a data-sourcepos=\"905:1-905:36\" href=\"https://elcomercio.pe\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">El Comercio</a> -\n<a data-sourcepos=\"906:1-906:30\" href=\"https://gestion.pe\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Gestión</a></p>\n<h5 id=\"user-content-uruguay\" data-sourcepos=\"907:1-907:13\" dir=\"auto\">Uruguay<a href=\"#uruguay\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Uruguay“\" data-heading-content=\"Uruguay\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h5>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"908:1-910:36\" dir=\"auto\"><a data-sourcepos=\"908:1-908:48\" href=\"https://www.elobservador.com.uy\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">El Observador</a> -\n<a data-sourcepos=\"909:1-909:37\" href=\"https://www.elpais.com.uy\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">El País</a> -\n<a data-sourcepos=\"910:1-910:36\" href=\"https://ladiaria.com.uy\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">La Diaria</a></p>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"912:1-912:23\" dir=\"auto\"><em data-sourcepos=\"912:1-912:23\">* free articles only.</em></p>\n<h3 id=\"user-content-sites-with-limited-number-of-free-articles\" data-sourcepos=\"914:1-914:46\" dir=\"auto\">Sites with limited number of free articles<a href=\"#sites-with-limited-number-of-free-articles\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Sites with limited number of free articles“\" data-heading-content=\"Sites with limited number of free articles\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h3>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"915:1-917:73\" dir=\"auto\">The free article limit can normally be bypassed by removing cookies for the site.<br data-sourcepos=\"915:82-915:84\">\nClick on the BPC-icon and then 'clear cookies'-button in the popup (for unsupported sites grant permission for domain).<br data-sourcepos=\"916:120-916:122\">\nIf removing the cookies works you can also add the site as a custom site.</p>\n<h3 id=\"user-content-new-site-requests\" data-sourcepos=\"919:1-919:21\" dir=\"auto\">New site requests<a href=\"#new-site-requests\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „New site requests“\" data-heading-content=\"New site requests\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h3>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"920:1-922:167\" dir=\"auto\">You can <a data-sourcepos=\"920:9-920:115\" href=\"https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean/-/issues\">submit a request for a new website</a>.<br data-sourcepos=\"920:117-920:119\">\nPlease use the issue template, read the following instructions and share your results for a quicker process.<br data-sourcepos=\"921:109-921:111\">\nRemember to check the <a data-sourcepos=\"922:23-922:132\" href=\"https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean/-/issues?scope=all&amp;state=all\">previous requests</a> before asking for a new website.</p>\n<ol data-sourcepos=\"923:1-928:32\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"923:1-923:79\">Open incognito window and search for article in Google search (or webcache).</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"924:1-924:157\">Clear cookies for the site (by this extension: opt-in to custom sites or grant permission for the site; also enables blocking of general paywall scripts).</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"925:1-925:81\">Disable Javascript on the site (by browser, uBlock Origin or other extension).</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"926:1-926:57\">Add the domain as custom site for more bypass options.</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"927:1-927:54\">Open page in reader view (by browser or extension).</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"928:1-929:0\">Try one of the archive sites.</li>\n</ol>\n<h3 id=\"user-content-add-custom-site\" data-sourcepos=\"930:1-930:19\" dir=\"auto\">Add custom site<a href=\"#add-custom-site\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Add custom site“\" data-heading-content=\"Add custom site\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h3>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"931:1-933:310\" dir=\"auto\">Add your own custom site (also for testing).<br data-sourcepos=\"931:45-931:47\">\nCheck 'Options'-link in popup-menu and go to custom sites.<br data-sourcepos=\"932:59-932:61\">\n*  by default BPC has limited permissions, but you can opt-in to enable custom sites (and also clear cookies/block general paywall-scripts for unlisted sites). You can also just request permissions for the custom sites you added yourself (or <code data-sourcepos=\"933:244-933:258\">clear cookies</code> (BPC-icon) to ask for permission for current site).</p>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"935:1-935:119\" dir=\"auto\">By default sites' cookies/local storage are blocked/removed (for example to bypass article limit when metered paywall).</p>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"937:1-937:26\" dir=\"auto\">Additional custom options:</p>\n<ul data-sourcepos=\"938:1-949:66\" dir=\"auto\">\n<li data-sourcepos=\"938:1-938:65\">allow/remove cookies (no options selected: cookies are blocked)</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"939:1-939:52\">set useragent to Googlebot, Bingbot or Facebookbot</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"940:1-940:77\">set referer (to Facebook, Google or Twitter; ignored when Googlebot is set)</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"941:1-941:23\">set random ip-address</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"942:1-942:102\">disable Javascript for (sub)domain(s), external domains (when host permission) and/or inline scripts</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"943:1-943:64\">block regular expression (to block specific script and/or xhr)</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"944:1-944:22\">unhide text amp-page</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"945:1-945:45\">redirect to amp-page when paywall(selector)</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"946:1-946:52\">load text from json when paywall|article(selector)</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"947:1-947:63\">load text from Google webcache when paywall|article(selector)</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"948:1-948:66\">add external link to archive-site when paywall|article(selector)</li>\n<li data-sourcepos=\"949:1-949:66\">remove/unhide elements in dom (optional for dev; check examples)</li>\n</ul>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"951:1-951:257\" dir=\"auto\"><a data-sourcepos=\"951:1-951:131\" href=\"https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean/-/blob/master/custom/sites_custom.json\">Example list of custom sites</a> or <a data-sourcepos=\"951:136-951:257\" href=\"https://gitlab.com/magnolia1234/bypass-paywalls-chrome-clean/-/raw/master/custom/sites_custom.json\">download list (json)</a></p>\n<h3 id=\"user-content-add-excluded-site\" data-sourcepos=\"953:1-953:21\" dir=\"auto\">Add excluded site<a href=\"#add-excluded-site\" aria-label=\"Link zur Überschrift „Add excluded site“\" data-heading-content=\"Add excluded site\" class=\"anchor\"></a></h3>\n<p data-sourcepos=\"954:1-955:67\" dir=\"auto\">Add excluded sites/domains (for your subscriptions).<br
